sections.RelicsRight:Toggle({
    Name = "Auto Relic Pick & Equip",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(v)
        _AO.AutoRelicEnabled = v
    end
}, "AutoRelicToggle")

sections.RelicsRight:Toggle({
    Name = "Replace With Better Relic",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(v)
        _AO.RelicUpgradeSwapEnabled = v
    end
}, "RelicUpgradeSwapToggle")

sections.RelicsRight:Paragraph({
    Header = "Replace Mode",
    Body = "When all slots are full:\n\nGoes through heroes from highest slot priority to lowest. On each hero, finds the worst equipped relic (lowest type value, then lowest roll). Replaces it if the new relic has higher type value, or same type value but better roll.\n\nRespects the allowed types filter below."
})

sections.RelicsRight:Divider()

-- RIGHT: Slot equip priority
sections.RelicsRight:Header({ Text = "Hero Slot Priority" })

sections.RelicsRight:Paragraph({
    Header = "Equip Order",
    Body = "Controls which hero gets relics first.\n\nYour team has 6 slots. Slot 1 is your first hero, Slot 6 is your last. Higher number on the slider = that hero gets relics before others.\n\nSet to 0 to skip a hero completely — no relics will be equipped on them.\n\nIf two heroes have the same priority, the one with fewer relics goes first."
})

for i = 1, 6 do
    sections.RelicsRight:Slider({
        Name = "Slot " .. i,
        Default = 6 - i + 1,
        Minimum = 0,
        Maximum = 10,
        Precision = 0,
        DisplayMethod = "Value",
        Callback = function(v)
            _AO.RelicSlotPriorities[i] = v
        end
    }, "RelicSlotPrio_" .. i)
end

sections.RelicsRight:Divider()

-- RIGHT: Allowed relic types per slot
sections.RelicsRight:Header({ Text = "Allowed Relics Per Slot" })

sections.RelicsRight:Paragraph({
    Header = "Type Filter",
    Body = "Choose which relic types each hero is allowed to receive.\n\nEmpty = accept any type (no filter).\nSelected = only those types can be equipped on that hero.\n\nExample: Slot 1 set to [DMG, Crit Mult] — that hero will only get Stinger or Demon Horn relics. Other types skip to the next hero."
})

for i = 1, 6 do
    sections.RelicsRight:Dropdown({
        Name = "Slot " .. i .. " allowed types",
        Multi = true,
        Options = RelicStatNames,
        Callback = function(selected)
            local allowed = {}
            for statName, isOn in pairs(selected) do
                if isOn and RelicStatToTier[statName] then
                    allowed[RelicStatToTier[statName]] = true
                end
            end
            _AO.RelicSlotAllowedTypes[i] = allowed
        end
    }, "RelicSlotTypes_" .. i)
end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════
-- AUTO RELIC PICK & EQUIP (Empty Throne raid, Game Stage only)
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════
if not isLobby then
    local relicOk, relicErr = pcall(function()
        local gamemodesNet = require(RS:WaitForChild("gameClient"):WaitForChild("net"):WaitForChild("gamemodesNet"))
        local FEECS = require(RS:WaitForChild("Packages"):WaitForChild("FEECS"))
        local relicsConfig = require(RS:WaitForChild("gameShared"):WaitForChild("config"):WaitForChild("relics"))
        local selectTowerStat = require(
            RS:WaitForChild("gameShared"):WaitForChild("store"):WaitForChild("slices")
              :WaitForChild("towers"):WaitForChild("selectors"):WaitForChild("selectTowerStat")
        )
        local resolveTowerEquippedRelics = require(
            RS:WaitForChild("gameShared"):WaitForChild("utilities"):WaitForChild("resolveTowerEquippedRelics")
        )
        local getEmptyThroneRelicConfig = require(
            RS:WaitForChild("gameShared"):WaitForChild("utilities"):WaitForChild("getEmptyThroneRelicConfig")
        )
        local itemsConfig = require(RS:WaitForChild("shared"):WaitForChild("config"):WaitForChild("items"))
        local myUserId = tostring(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.UserId)

        -- Farm heroes detection via game config (heroType == "farm")
        local function isFarmHero(heroId)
            if not heroId then return false end
            local cfg = itemsConfig.hero.get(heroId)
            return cfg and cfg.heroType == "farm"
        end

        local function parseRelicId(relicId)
            -- Format: "dynamicRelic:<tierLetter>:<rarity>:<value>"
            local parsed = relicsConfig.get(relicId)
            if parsed then
                return parsed.tier, parsed.rarity, parsed.rolledValue, parsed
            end
            return nil, nil, nil, nil
        end

        local function relicMeetsThreshold(relicId)
            local tier, _, value = parseRelicId(relicId)
            if not tier or not value then return true end -- unknown relic = accept
            local minVal = _AO.RelicMinThresholds[tier] or 0
            return value >= minVal
        end

        local function pickBestRelic(relicIds)
            -- Pick relic with highest value above threshold
            local best = nil
            local bestVal = -1
            for _, rid in ipairs(relicIds) do
                local tier, _, value = parseRelicId(rid)
                if tier and value then
                    local minVal = _AO.RelicMinThresholds[tier] or 0
                    if value >= minVal and value > bestVal then
                        bestVal = value
                        best = rid
                    end
                end
            end
            return best
        end

        -- Check if a relic tier is allowed on a given slot
        local function isTierAllowedOnSlot(tier, slot)
            local allowed = _AO.RelicSlotAllowedTypes[slot]
            if not allowed or not next(allowed) then return true end -- empty = allow all
            return allowed[tier] == true
        end

        local function getMyTowers()
            local towers = {}
            local heroSlots = {}
            pcall(function()
                local state = gameClientStore:getState()
                if state and state.data and state.data.heroes then
                    local heroes = state.data.heroes[myUserId]
                    if type(heroes) == "table" then
                        for uuid, hero in pairs(heroes) do
                            if type(hero) == "table" and type(hero.equipped) == "number" and hero.equipped > 0 then
                                heroSlots[uuid] = hero.equipped
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
            for entityId, etype in FEECS.queryEntities("entityType") do
                if etype == "towerEntity" then
                    local comp = FEECS.getAllEntityComponents(entityId)
                    if comp and comp.owner == myUserId then
                        local heroId = comp.id
                        local isFarm = isFarmHero(heroId)
                        local towerUid = comp.uniqueId
                        local slot = heroSlots[comp.originalUniqueId] or 999
                        local relicId = gameClientStore and gameClientStore:getState(selectTowerStat(towerUid, "relicId"))
                        local relicData = gameClientStore and gameClientStore:getState(selectTowerStat(towerUid, "relicEquippedData"))
                        local equipped = resolveTowerEquippedRelics.resolveIds(relicId, relicData)
                        table.insert(towers, {
                            uniqueId = towerUid,
                            heroId = heroId,
                            heroName = comp.id and (itemsConfig.hero.get(comp.id) or {}).name or "Unknown",
                            isFarm = isFarm,
                            slot = slot,
                            relicCount = #equipped,
                            equippedRelics = equipped,
                        })
                    end
                end
            end
            table.sort(towers, function(a, b) return a.slot < b.slot end)
            return towers
        end

        local function findBestTower(towers, maxRelics, relicTier)
            -- Highest slot priority FIRST, then fewest relics.
            -- Slot priority 0 = skip. Checks allowed types filter.
            local best = nil
            local bestSlotPrio = -1
            local bestCount = maxRelics + 1
            for _, t in ipairs(towers) do
                local slotPrio = _AO.RelicSlotPriorities[t.slot] or 0
                if not t.isFarm and slotPrio > 0 and t.relicCount < maxRelics then
                    if relicTier and not isTierAllowedOnSlot(relicTier, t.slot) then
                        -- relic type not allowed on this slot, skip
                    elseif slotPrio > bestSlotPrio or (slotPrio == bestSlotPrio and t.relicCount < bestCount) then
                        bestSlotPrio = slotPrio
                        bestCount = t.relicCount
                        best = t
                    end
                end
            end
            return best
        end

        local function findWorstRelicToReplace(towers, newRelicId)
            -- Walk towers by slot priority (highest first).
            -- On each: check allowed types, find worst by type priority then value.
            -- Replace if new relic is more valuable (higher type prio, or same prio + higher roll).
            local newTier, _, newValue = parseRelicId(newRelicId)
            if not newTier or not newValue then return nil, nil end
            local newPrio = _AO.RelicTypePriorities[newTier] or 5

            local sorted = {}
            for _, t in ipairs(towers) do
                if not t.isFarm then
                    local slotPrio = _AO.RelicSlotPriorities[t.slot] or 0
                    if slotPrio > 0 and #t.equippedRelics > 0 and isTierAllowedOnSlot(newTier, t.slot) then
                        table.insert(sorted, { tower = t, slotPrio = slotPrio })
                    end
                end
            end
            table.sort(sorted, function(a, b) return a.slotPrio > b.slotPrio end)

            for _, entry in ipairs(sorted) do
                local t = entry.tower
                local worstId = nil
                local worstPrio = math.huge
                local worstVal = math.huge
                for _, eqRelicId in ipairs(t.equippedRelics) do
                    local eqTier, _, eqValue = parseRelicId(eqRelicId)
                    if eqTier and eqValue then
                        local eqPrio = _AO.RelicTypePriorities[eqTier] or 5
                        if eqPrio < worstPrio or (eqPrio == worstPrio and eqValue < worstVal) then
                            worstPrio = eqPrio
                            worstVal = eqValue
                            worstId = eqRelicId
                        end
                    end
                end
                if worstId then
                    if newPrio > worstPrio or (newPrio == worstPrio and newValue > worstVal) then
                        return t, worstId
                    end
                end
            end
            return nil, nil
        end

        -- Helper: call ZAP .call() with timeout (same pattern as macro playback)
        local function zapCallWithTimeout(fn, timeout)
            timeout = timeout or 5
            local callDone = false
            local callOk, callResult, callErr = false, nil, nil
            task.spawn(function()
                callOk, callResult, callErr = pcall(fn)
                callDone = true
            end)
            local waitStart = tick()
            while not callDone and (tick() - waitStart < timeout) do
                task.wait(0.1)
            end
            if not callDone then
                return false, nil, "TIMEOUT (" .. timeout .. "s)"
            end
            return callOk, callResult, callErr
        end

        -- Listen for relic selection offer (server sends 2 relics to choose from)
        gamemodesNet.showEmptyThroneRelics.on(function(_, dropId, relicIds)
            dbg("Relic OFFER received: dropId=" .. tostring(dropId) .. " relicIds=" .. tostring(relicIds and #relicIds or "nil") .. " enabled=" .. tostring(_AO.AutoRelicEnabled))
            if not _AO.AutoRelicEnabled or not getgenv()._AORunning then
                dbg("Relic OFFER: SKIPPED (disabled)")
                return
            end
            if not relicIds or #relicIds == 0 then
                dbg("Relic OFFER: SKIPPED (empty relicIds)")
                return
            end

            for i, rid in ipairs(relicIds) do
                local tier, rarity, value = parseRelicId(rid)
                local minVal = _AO.RelicMinThresholds[tier] or 0
                dbg("  [" .. i .. "] " .. tostring(tier) .. " " .. tostring(rarity) .. " val=" .. tostring(value) .. " minThresh=" .. tostring(minVal))
            end

            local chosen = pickBestRelic(relicIds)
            if not chosen then
                dbg("Relic OFFER: pickBestRelic=nil (all filtered), picking first")
                chosen = relicIds[1]
            else
                local cTier, _, cVal = parseRelicId(chosen)
                dbg("Relic OFFER: picked " .. tostring(cTier) .. " val=" .. tostring(cVal))
            end

            task.wait(0.3)
            local ok, result, err = zapCallWithTimeout(function()
                return gamemodesNet.selectEmptyThroneRelic.call(chosen)
            end, 5)
            dbg("Relic SELECT: ok=" .. tostring(ok) .. " result=" .. tostring(result) .. " err=" .. tostring(err))
        end)

        -- Listen for relic drop spawn (after selection, item appears in world)
        gamemodesNet.spawnEmptyThroneRelicDrop.on(function(dropData)
            dbg("Relic SPAWN received: id=" .. tostring(dropData and dropData.id or "nil") .. " enabled=" .. tostring(_AO.AutoRelicEnabled))
            if not _AO.AutoRelicEnabled or not getgenv()._AORunning then
                dbg("Relic SPAWN: SKIPPED (disabled)")
                return
            end
            if not dropData then return end

            local dropId = dropData.id
            local relicId = dropData.relicId
            local flyDuration = dropData.dropDuration or 1
            local endPos = dropData.endPosition

            local tier, rarity, value = parseRelicId(relicId)
            local minVal = tier and (_AO.RelicMinThresholds[tier] or 0) or "?"
            dbg("Relic SPAWN: " .. tostring(tier) .. " " .. tostring(rarity) .. " val=" .. tostring(value) .. " minThresh=" .. tostring(minVal) .. " fly=" .. tostring(flyDuration) .. "s")

            if not relicMeetsThreshold(relicId) then
                dbg("Relic SPAWN: DISCARDING (val " .. tostring(value) .. " < threshold " .. tostring(minVal) .. ")")
                task.wait(0.5)
                zapCallWithTimeout(function()
                    return gamemodesNet.discardEmptyThroneRelicDrop.call(dropId)
                end, 5)
                return
            end

            -- Wait for relic to fully land
            task.wait(flyDuration + 1.5)
            if not _AO.AutoRelicEnabled or not getgenv()._AORunning then return end

            local config = getEmptyThroneRelicConfig("emptyThrone")
            local maxRelics = config and config.maxRelicsPerTower or 2
            dbg("Relic: maxRelics=" .. tostring(maxRelics))

            local towers = getMyTowers()
            dbg("Relic: Found " .. #towers .. " own towers:")
            for ti, t in ipairs(towers) do
                dbg("  [" .. ti .. "] " .. tostring(t.heroName) .. " uid=" .. tostring(t.uniqueId)
                    .. " slot=" .. tostring(t.slot) .. " slotPrio=" .. tostring(_AO.RelicSlotPriorities[t.slot] or 0) .. " farm=" .. tostring(t.isFarm) .. " relics=" .. tostring(t.relicCount))
            end

            local target = findBestTower(towers, maxRelics, tier)

            if not target then
                if _AO.RelicUpgradeSwapEnabled then
                    local swapTower, swapRelicId = findWorstRelicToReplace(towers, relicId)
                    if swapTower and swapRelicId then
                        dbg("Relic swap: replacing " .. tostring(swapRelicId) .. " on " .. tostring(swapTower.heroName))
                        -- Teleport to relic, equip, teleport back
                        local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                        local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local savedCF = hrp and hrp.CFrame
                        if hrp and endPos then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(endPos + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0))
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        local ok, result, err = zapCallWithTimeout(function()
                            return gamemodesNet.openEmptyThroneRelicDrop.call(dropId, swapTower.uniqueId, swapRelicId)
                        end, 5)
                        dbg("Relic swap: ok=" .. tostring(ok) .. " result=" .. tostring(result) .. " err=" .. tostring(err))
                        if hrp and savedCF and hrp.Parent then
                            task.wait(0.15)
                            hrp.CFrame = savedCF
                        end
                        return
                    else
                        dbg("Relic: new relic not better than any equipped, discarding")
                    end
                else
                    dbg("Relic: no tower with free slot (swap disabled), discarding")
                end
                zapCallWithTimeout(function()
                    return gamemodesNet.discardEmptyThroneRelicDrop.call(dropId)
                end, 5)
                return
            end

            dbg("Relic EQUIP: target=" .. tostring(target.heroName) .. " uid=" .. target.uniqueId .. " slot=" .. tostring(target.slot) .. " slotPrio=" .. tostring(_AO.RelicSlotPriorities[target.slot] or 0) .. " relics=" .. tostring(target.relicCount))

            -- Teleport to relic drop position
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local savedCF = hrp and hrp.CFrame

            if hrp and endPos then
                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(endPos + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0))
                dbg("Relic: teleported to drop")
                task.wait(0.5)
            end

            -- Equip via ZAP .call() with timeout
            local ok, result, err = zapCallWithTimeout(function()
                return gamemodesNet.openEmptyThroneRelicDrop.call(dropId, target.uniqueId, "")
            end, 5)
            dbg("Relic equip: ok=" .. tostring(ok) .. " result=" .. tostring(result) .. " err=" .. tostring(err))

            -- Verify
            task.wait(0.5)
            local towersAfter = getMyTowers()
            for _, t in ipairs(towersAfter) do
                if t.uniqueId == target.uniqueId then
                    dbg("Relic: VERIFY " .. t.heroName .. " relics=" .. t.relicCount .. " (was " .. target.relicCount .. ")")
                    break
                end
            end

            -- Teleport back
            if hrp and savedCF and hrp.Parent then
                hrp.CFrame = savedCF
                dbg("Relic: teleported back")
            end
        end)

        -- Handle invalidation (relic expired)
        gamemodesNet.invalidateEmptyThroneRelicDrop.on(function(dropId)
            dbg("Relic INVALIDATED: " .. tostring(dropId))
        end)

        -- Log current settings
        local typeDump = {}
        for _, r in ipairs(AllRelics) do
            table.insert(typeDump, r.stat .. "=" .. tostring(_AO.RelicTypePriorities[r.tier]))
        end
        local slotDump = {}
        for i = 1, 6 do
            local allowed = _AO.RelicSlotAllowedTypes[i]
            local filter = (allowed and next(allowed)) and "filtered" or "any"
            table.insert(slotDump, "s" .. i .. "=prio" .. tostring(_AO.RelicSlotPriorities[i]) .. "(" .. filter .. ")")
        end
        dbg("Relic INIT OK: TypeVal=[" .. table.concat(typeDump, ",") .. "] Slots=[" .. table.concat(slotDump, ", ") .. "]")
    end)
    if not relicOk then
        warn("[AH] Relic init FAILED: " .. tostring(relicErr))
    end
end

sections.AutoRight:Toggle({

    Default = false,

}, "WebhookEnabledToggle")

Set Discord User ID to get @pinged.\n\nPriority: Return Lobby > Next > Replay\nOnly one can be active."
})

-- Auto Vending + Gold Shop + Chain Shop (Lobby only)
-- Wrapped in IIFE: Luau limits ~200 locals per chunk; this file is one chunk.
; (function()
local AutoVendingEnabled = false
local AutoGoldShopEnabled = false
local GoldShopSelectedItems = {} -- {itemIndex = true}
local AutoChainShopEnabled = false
local ChainShopSelectedItems = {} -- {name = true}

-- Build gold shop item list from config
local GoldShopItems = {} -- {index, id, name, cost, stock, currency}
pcall(function()
    local shopConfig = require(RS:WaitForChild("shared"):WaitForChild("config"):WaitForChild("shops"):WaitForChild("speedwagonShop"))
    for idx, item in pairs(shopConfig) do
        if type(item) == "table" and item.id then
            table.insert(GoldShopItems, {
                index = item.index or idx,
                id = item.id,
                name = item.name or item.id,
                cost = item.cost or 0,
                stock = item.stock or 1,
                currency = item.currency or "token",
                rotation = item.rotationPeriod or "permanent",
            })
        end
    end
    table.sort(GoldShopItems, function(a, b) return a.index < b.index end)
end)

-- Build chain of control shop item list from config
local ChainShopItems = {}
pcall(function()
    local shopConfig = require(RS:WaitForChild("shared"):WaitForChild("config"):WaitForChild("shops"):WaitForChild("chainsOfControlShop"))
    for idx, item in pairs(shopConfig) do
        if type(item) == "table" and item.id then
            table.insert(ChainShopItems, {
                index = item.index or idx,
                id = item.id,
                name = item.name or item.id,
                cost = item.cost or 0,
                stock = item.stock or 1,
                currency = item.currency or "bloodiedChains",
                rotation = item.rotationPeriod or "permanent",
            })
        end
    end
    table.sort(ChainShopItems, function(a, b) return a.index < b.index end)
end)

local function GetChainShopDisplayNames()
    local names = {}
    for _, item in ipairs(ChainShopItems) do
        table.insert(names, item.name .. " (" .. tostring(item.cost) .. "bc)")
    end
    if #names == 0 then table.insert(names, "None") end
    return names
end

local function GetGoldShopDisplayNames()
    local names = {}
    for _, item in ipairs(GoldShopItems) do
        local cur = item.currency == "gold" and "g" or "t"
        table.insert(names, item.name .. " (" .. tostring(item.cost) .. cur .. ")")
    end
    if #names == 0 then table.insert(names, "None") end
    return names
end

-- Get remaining stock for a shop item (speedwagon)
local function GetShopStock(itemIndex)
    if not clientStore then return 0 end
    local ok, state = pcall(function() return clientStore:getState() end)
    if not ok or not state or not state.data or not state.data.speedwagonShop then return 0 end
    local shop = state.data.speedwagonShop[userId]
    if not shop or not shop.stock then return 999 end
    local stockData = shop.stock[itemIndex]
    if not stockData then return 999 end
    return stockData.remaining or 0
end

-- Get remaining stock for a chain of control shop item
local function GetChainShopStock(itemIndex)
    if not clientStore then return 0 end
    local ok, state = pcall(function() return clientStore:getState() end)
    if not ok or not state or not state.data or not state.data.chainOfControlShop then return 0 end
    local shop = state.data.chainOfControlShop[userId]
    if not shop or not shop.stock then return 999 end
    local stockData = shop.stock[itemIndex]
    if not stockData then return 999 end
    return stockData.remaining or 0
end

-- Get vending claims for a machine
local function GetVendingClaims(machineId)
    if not clientStore then return 0 end
    local ok, state = pcall(function() return clientStore:getState() end)
    if not ok or not state or not state.data or not state.data.vendingMachines then return 0 end
    local vm = state.data.vendingMachines[userId]
    if not vm or not vm.claims then return 0 end
    return vm.claims[machineId] or 0
end

-- Auto Vending Loop
task.spawn(function()
    while getgenv()._AORunning do
        if AutoVendingEnabled and isLobby and _AO.ModulesLoaded and playerNet then
            pcall(function()
                local CS = game:GetService("CollectionService")
                local machines = CS:GetTagged("vendingMachine")
                dbg("Vending: found " .. #machines .. " machines")
                for _, machine in pairs(machines) do
                    if not AutoVendingEnabled or not getgenv()._AORunning then break end
                    local machineId = machine:GetAttribute("vendingMachineId")
                    dbg("Vending: machine=" .. tostring(machine) .. " machineId=" .. tostring(machineId))
                    if machineId then
                        machineId = tostring(machineId)
                        local claims = GetVendingClaims(machineId)
                        dbg("Vending: machineId=" .. machineId .. " claims=" .. tostring(claims))
                        if claims < 5 then
                            -- Teleport to machine
                            local hrp = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local target = machine:IsA("BasePart") and machine or machine:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
                            if hrp and target then
                                hrp.CFrame = target.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                            while claims < 5 and AutoVendingEnabled and getgenv()._AORunning do
                                local ok, result = pcall(function()
                                    return playerNet.useVendingMachine.call(machineId)
                                end)
                                dbg("Vending: call ok=" .. tostring(ok) .. " result=" .. tostring(result))
                                if ok and result then
                                    claims = claims + 1
                                    task.wait(1.5)
                                else
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
        task.wait(10)
    end
end)

-- Auto Gold Shop Loop
task.spawn(function()
    while getgenv()._AORunning do
        if AutoGoldShopEnabled and isLobby and _AO.ModulesLoaded then
            dbg("GoldShop: loop tick, items=" .. #GoldShopItems .. " selected:")
            for k in pairs(GoldShopSelectedItems) do dbg("  selected: '" .. k .. "'") end
            pcall(function()
                local coreNet = require(RS:WaitForChild("lobbyClient"):WaitForChild("net"):WaitForChild("core"))
                for _, item in ipairs(GoldShopItems) do
                    if not AutoGoldShopEnabled or not getgenv()._AORunning then break end
                    local cur = item.currency == "gold" and "g" or "t"
                    local displayName = item.name .. " (" .. tostring(item.cost) .. cur .. ")"
                    dbg("GoldShop: checking '" .. displayName .. "' selected=" .. tostring(GoldShopSelectedItems[displayName] or false))
                    if GoldShopSelectedItems[displayName] then
                        local stock = GetShopStock(item.index)
                        dbg("GoldShop: " .. item.id .. " stock=" .. tostring(stock))
                        while stock > 0 and AutoGoldShopEnabled and getgenv()._AORunning do
                            local ok, result = pcall(function()
                                return coreNet.speedwagonPurchase.call(item.id, 1)
                            end)
                            dbg("GoldShop: purchase " .. item.id .. " ok=" .. tostring(ok) .. " result=" .. tostring(result))
                            if ok and result then
                                stock = stock - 1
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            else
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
        task.wait(5)
    end
end)

; (function()
local AutoCraftStarsEnabled = false

local STAR_RECIPES = {
    { pure = "redStarPure",    impure = "redStarImpure"    },
    { pure = "blueStarPure",   impure = "blueStarImpure"   },
    { pure = "purpleStarPure", impure = "purpleStarImpure" },
    { pure = "greenStarPure",  impure = "greenStarImpure"  },
    { pure = "pinkStarPure",   impure = "pinkStarImpure"   },
    { pure = "yellowStarPure", impure = "yellowStarImpure" },
}

task.spawn(function()
    while getgenv()._AORunning do
        if AutoCraftStarsEnabled and isLobby and _AO.ModulesLoaded then
            pcall(function()
                local collectionNet = require(RS:WaitForChild("lobbyClient"):WaitForChild("net"):WaitForChild("collection"))
                local state = clientStore:getState()
                local col = SumCollectionByItemId(state)

                for _, star in ipairs(STAR_RECIPES) do
                    if not AutoCraftStarsEnabled or not getgenv()._AORunning then break end
                    local pureCount = col[star.pure] or 0
                    if pureCount < 100 then
                        local impureCount = col[star.impure] or 0
                        local needed = 100 - pureCount
                        local canCraft = math.min(needed, math.floor(impureCount / 3))
                        dbg("CraftStars: " .. star.pure .. " have=" .. pureCount .. " impure=" .. impureCount .. " canCraft=" .. canCraft)
                        for _ = 1, canCraft do
                            if not AutoCraftStarsEnabled or not getgenv()._AORunning then break end
                            local ok, result = pcall(function()
                                return collectionNet.craftRecipe.call(star.pure)
                            end)
                            dbg("CraftStars: craft " .. star.pure .. " ok=" .. tostring(ok) .. " result=" .. tostring(result))
                            if not ok or not result then break end
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        -- refresh counts after crafting a color
                        if canCraft > 0 then
                            state = clientStore:getState()
                            col = SumCollectionByItemId(state)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
        task.wait(5)
    end
end)
